msg:During the National Day holiday, I took my parents and daughter to travel around. Friends who asked Sanming recommended Meiyuan International. Good location, easy to go anywhere.
We arrived at night, and the room layout was very interesting. Although it is not a new hotel, the general facilities are well maintained, and the bedding is clean and tidy. For those of us who take a baby out, try not to choose a new hotel to avoid the smell.
It is particularly worth mentioning that the buffet restaurant in Meiyuan is really cost-effective. highly recommended!
The coupon for the small program group I used for the lunch buffet is particularly cost-effective, only 60 yuan per person. There are many varieties of vegetables, such as plum garden sauce duck, plum garden jasper rolls, freshly fried cowboy bones and cod fish, southern suckling pig knuckle, leek flower river prawns; the staple food is sweet potato corn bun fried noodles (that sweet potato is super delicious); the stew pot actually has it. Golden thread lotus! There are also freshly cut beef, mutton, sea cucumber and shellfish that can be blanched in hot pot, live seafood only has shrimps at noon, and one person and a medium-sized abalone. There are so many that I canâ€™t remember. But compared to the 200-300 yuan we spent in other places before, there are few dishes, this is too worthwhile. Mom and Dad are very satisfied. I heard that there are more dinner dishes. There are live crabs, so I must try again next time.
By the way, the chef who cuts the sauced duck is very good. He saw me holding my daughter. I cut a big duck leg for her, my daughter is so happy, thank you!
When I went out early in the morning, I came back and the family had a nice meal at the buffet and then went upstairs to rest. It was perfect.
In middle age, when we come out to play, our parents are happy, and our daughter is happy, and we are happy. Next time I come to Sanming, I will choose Meiyuan.
